# Quality Constitution: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Purpose
Quality in ZINC-FUSION-V16 means buyer-facing soybean oil procurement decisions are grounded in accurate, traceable, and operationally consistent data contracts across Supabase, API routes, dashboard rendering, and training gates.

Deming applies here as contract integrity built into route code, schema contracts, and quality artifacts before later review phases. Juran applies as fitness for procurement use: the system must preserve fallback behavior, route-envelope stability, and approval-gated model operations so Chris and Kevin do not consume misleading outputs. Crosby applies because preventing silent contract drift (status vocab mismatch, hidden overlay disablement, envelope divergence) is lower cost than downstream outage analysis and procurement mis-timing.

## Coverage Targets
| Subsystem | Target | Why |
| --- | --- | --- |
| "'`app/api/zl/*` forecast and intraday routes | 92% | These routes carry price, target-zone, and fallback contracts directly into decision surfaces; parity gaps are already observed in exploration. |
| `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx` and dashboard wiring | 90% | Target-zone visibility can be disabled even when data is present; this is high-impact on user interpretation. |
| `lib/server/*` ingest/snapshot/trusted-source utilities | 88% | Status normalization and trusted-source allowlists are cross-cutting and can silently drift. |
| `python/fusion/*` train/promote/pipeline gate paths | 90% | Explicit approval gates are a hard safety boundary for model execution and cloud promotion. |
| `supabase/migrations/*` ops and mkt contract tables | 85% | Schema-level vocabulary and fallback tables define runtime behavior and observability semantics. |
| `docs/*` operator-facing startup and policy docs | 75% | Documentation parity matters for operational correctness but is lower runtime criticality than core code paths. |

## Coverage Theater Prevention
The following are non-compliant test patterns for this repository:

- Asserting only HTTP status without validating payload contract fields (`ok`, `data`, `asOf`, `source`) where envelope semantics are required.
- Asserting that forecast/target arrays are non-empty without proving horizon normalization and per-route parity behavior.
- Testing ingestion telemetry by checking row existence only, without validating canonical status vocabulary alignment across SQL and TS writers.
- Testing chart rendering by mounting the component only, without checking that forecast-target overlay attachment path is enabled when target-zone data exists.
- Testing training gates by asserting dry-run returns a dict, without asserting non-approved non-dry behavior is blocked.
- Treating README existence as documentation quality; tests must assert repo policy alignment on prohibited hardcoded port guidance.

## Fitness-to-Purpose Scenarios
### Scenario 1: Intraday Fallback Contract Drift
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-001]

**What happened:** `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts` states a 15-minute then 1-minute fallback contract but currently executes only `mkt.price_15m` and always emits `source: "mkt.price_15m"`. During sparse 15-minute data windows, this permits empty/stale intraday payloads while a populated 1-minute table exists.

**The requirement:** Intraday route behavior must execute documented fallback semantics and emit source metadata that reflects the actual query path.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementTests.test_req_001_intraday_route_contains_executable_1m_fallback`

### Scenario 2: Invisible Target Zones Despite Available Data
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-002]

**What happened:** Dashboard page fetches `targetZones` and passes them to `ZlCandlestickChart`, but `SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY = false` prevents `ForecastTargetsPrimitive` attachment. The architecture permits valid forecast-zone data to remain invisible to users.

**The requirement:** When target-zone data is supplied to chart boundary, overlay plumbing must be enabled or explicitly replaced by an equivalent visible projection.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.FitnessScenarioTests.test_scenario_2_forecast_overlay_gate_is_not_hard_disabled`

### Scenario 3: Divergent Forecast Target API Envelopes
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-002]

**What happened:** `/api/zl/target-zones` uses a typed envelope while `/api/zl/forecast-targets` uses `{asOfDate, targets}` and route-specific error shape. This permits parser duplication and inconsistent error handling across consumers of equivalent domain data.

**The requirement:** Forecast-target routes must share one canonical response envelope or provide explicit typed adapters documenting differences.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementTests.test_req_002_forecast_target_routes_share_api_envelope_contract`

### Scenario 4: Ingest Status Vocabulary Fragmentation
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-003]

**What happened:** SQL jobs write lower-case `running/ok/failed` while TS helper writes upper-case `RUNNING/SUCCESS/FAILED` to `ops.ingest_run.status`. This permits split analytics filters and inconsistent alert logic.

**The requirement:** All writers to `ops.ingest_run.status` must use one canonical status vocabulary.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementTests.test_req_003_ingest_status_vocab_is_canonical_across_writers`

### Scenario 5: Unauthorized Model Execution
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-004]

**What happened:** Train and promote phases are safety-critical operations. If approval gates are bypassed in non-dry runs, model artifacts or cloud tables can mutate without explicit operator authorization.

**The requirement:** Non-dry `train` and `promote` execution requires explicit approval and emits a blocking error when approval is absent.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementTests.test_req_004_train_phase_requires_explicit_approval`

### Scenario 6: Runtime External Pull Coupling on Read Paths
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-006]

**What happened:** AI-first routes still perform request-time trusted-market pulls before snapshot fallback. Third-party latency/outage can cascade into user-facing API delays.

**The requirement:** Runtime read-path external pulls must either be bounded with explicit fallback semantics or isolated behind snapshot-first behavior with clear degraded metadata.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.FitnessScenarioTests.test_scenario_6_routes_document_snapshot_and_trusted_pull_order`

### Scenario 7: Snapshot Trust Boundary Drift
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-004]

**What happened:** `TRUSTED_SNAPSHOT_SOURCES` defines a strict allowlist. If producers are added without allowlist updates, snapshots fail closed and AI cards silently lose expected data.

**The requirement:** Any new snapshot source identifier must be updated in the trust allowlist in the same change as producer wiring.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.BoundaryAndEdgeCaseTests.test_boundary_trusted_snapshot_sources_are_exactly_expected_set`

### Scenario 8: Operator Guidance Drift
**Requirement tag:** [Req: code-derived — REQ-012]

**What happened:** Root README includes starter-template startup guidance including localhost:3000 while authority docs prohibit hardcoded port assumptions. This can mislead operators and parity validation steps.

**The requirement:** Operator-facing docs must not reintroduce prohibited startup assumptions that conflict with V16 authority rules.

**How to verify:** `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.FitnessScenarioTests.test_scenario_8_readme_drift_is_detectable`

## AI Session Quality Discipline
1. Read `quality/QUALITY.md`, `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`, and `quality/COVERAGE_MATRIX.md` before modifying implementation.
2. Preserve `Pattern` fields on all pattern-tagged REQs in both markdown and manifest artifacts.
3. Do not modify files outside `quality/` during quality playbook phase execution.
4. For enumeration/allowlist claims, use mechanical extraction artifacts under `quality/mechanical/` before writing conclusions.
5. Run `quality/mechanical/verify.sh` after changing any requirement tied to enumeration or dispatch completeness.
6. Update `quality/PROGRESS.md` artifact inventory in the same change as generated artifact updates.

## The Human Gate
- Approving training and cloud promotion execution beyond dry-run gates.
- Accepting temporary contract divergence when external dependencies or release constraints require staged remediation.
- Deciding rollout timing for envelope-contract convergence across independently consumed API surfaces.
- Prioritizing UX tradeoffs for chart overlays and degraded-mode messaging under live-feed outages.

# Behavioral Contracts: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Extraction Scope
- Source basis: "'`quality/EXPLORATION.md` Phase 1 findings and cited code paths.
- Target areas: intraday/forecast API routes, chart rendering path, ingest telemetry writers, training and promotion gates, snapshot trust boundary, operator docs.

## Summary By Category
- `API`: 6
- `INVARIANT`: 5
- `LIFECYCLE`: 2
- `SECURITY`: 1
- `OBSERVABILITY`: 3
- `DOCS`: 1

## Contract Inventory
### `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts`
1. `[API]` `GET()` advertises a two-step fallback contract (15m then 1m) and must keep declaration and executable path aligned. (`app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:16-23`)
2. `[OBSERVABILITY]` `ApiEnvelope.source` must identify the actual table path used for response payload. (`app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:41-46`)

### `supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql`
3. `[INVARIANT]` `mkt.price_15m` and `mkt.price_1m` coexist as eligible intraday data sources; route behavior must remain consistent with this schema capability. (`supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql:18-19`)

### `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts` and `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts`
4. `[API]` Forecast-target surfaces represent the same domain payload and must converge on one stable envelope or explicit typed adapter contracts. (`app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:80-87`, `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:103-106`)
5. `[INVARIANT]` Horizon normalization behavior (`AG_HORIZON_DAYS`, `LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP`, `normalizeHorizon`) must remain equivalent across all forecast-target routes. (`app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:7-24`, `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:16-33`, `app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts:7-24`)

### `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx` and dashboard page wiring
6. `[API]` Chart receives `targetZones` from dashboard page and must render equivalent target-zone signal when data exists. (`app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx:12-33`, `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx:40`, `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx:257-269`)
7. `[LIFECYCLE]` Primitive attach/detach lifecycle must mirror feature gates to avoid silent rendering path disablement. (`components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx:253-266`, `components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx:332-337`)

### `ops.ingest_run` schema and writers
8. `[OBSERVABILITY]` All writers to `ops.ingest_run.status` must share one canonical status vocabulary for deterministic analytics and alerting. (`supabase/migrations/202603180009_ops_vegas.sql:3-8`, `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:3-4`, `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:55-57`)
9. `[LIFECYCLE]` Run lifecycle semantics (`start`, terminal success/failure, timestamps, records count) must preserve one run-id progression contract. (`lib/server/ingest-run.ts:6-26`, `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:28-61`)

### Training and promotion gates
10. `[SECURITY]` Non-dry training and cloud promotion execution is approval-gated; calls without explicit approval must fail closed. (`python/fusion/pipeline.py:46-58`, `python/fusion/train_models.py:770-773`, `python/fusion/promote_to_cloud.py:172-173`)
11. `[INVARIANT]` Pipeline phase dispatcher must preserve approval flags through `run_phase` boundary to downstream stage functions. (`python/fusion/pipeline.py:46-58`)

### Snapshot trust and external pull coupling
12. `[INVARIANT]` Snapshot intake requires metadata and trusted-source allowlist membership; untrusted identifiers fail closed. (`lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts:21-27`, `lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts:41-50`)
13. `[API]` AI-first card routes using runtime trusted-market pulls must maintain explicit fallback to snapshots and degraded-mode visibility when pulls fail. (`app/api/strategy/posture/route.ts:142-169`, `app/api/sentiment/overview/route.ts:188-193`, `lib/server/trusted-market-sources.ts:139-146`)

### Documentation alignment
14. `[DOCS]` Operator startup and environment instructions must align with V16 authority docs and avoid prohibited hardcoded-port assumptions. (`README.md:1-4`, `README.md:95`, `AGENTS.md:53`)

# Requirements: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Project Overview
These requirements are derived from "'`quality/EXPLORATION.md` Phase 1 findings and govern forecast route contracts, ingestion telemetry consistency, approval-gated model operations, runtime data-source resilience, and the canonical quality-artifact layout for this run.

## Requirements
### REQ-001: Intraday fallback execution parity
- Statement: `app/api/zl/intraday` must execute the declared 15m->1m fallback behavior when primary query returns no usable bars.
- Tier: 3
- Source type: code-derived
- Pattern: parity
- References:
  - `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:16-23`
  - `supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql:18-19`
- Linked use cases: `UC-1`
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  - `GET()` includes an executable branch that queries `mkt.price_1m` when `mkt.price_15m` produces no usable rows.
  - Response `source` reflects the table actually used for the payload.
  - Fallback behavior is mechanically testable by source-level contract assertions in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### REQ-002: Forecast-target envelope parity
- Statement: Forecast target endpoints must expose one stable envelope contract for equivalent semantic payloads.
- Tier: 3
- Source type: code-derived
- Pattern: parity
- References:
  - `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:80-87`
  - `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:103-106`
  - `components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx:62-83`
- Linked use cases: `UC-2.a`, `UC-2.b`
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  - `/api/zl/target-zones` and `/api/zl/forecast-targets` either emit the same envelope keys or publish explicit typed adapters consumed by all clients.
  - Success and error payload contracts are parsable by one canonical client-side adapter path.
  - Horizon normalization behavior remains equivalent across both routes.

### REQ-003: Canonical `ops.ingest_run.status` vocabulary
- Statement: All writers to `ops.ingest_run.status` must share one canonical status vocabulary.
- Tier: 3
- Source type: code-derived
- Pattern: compensation
- References:
  - `supabase/migrations/202603180009_ops_vegas.sql:3-8`
  - `supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:138-141`
  - `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:55-57`
  - `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:3-4`
- Linked use cases: `UC-3`
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  - SQL and TS writers use one status enum/value set.
  - Lifecycle writes (`start`, `success`, `failure`) remain query-consistent across producers.
  - Ops dashboards can filter by one status vocabulary without producer-specific translation.

### REQ-004: Explicit approval gate for non-dry training and promotion
- Statement: Training and cloud promotion execution requires explicit approval in non-dry runs.
- Tier: 3
- Source type: code-derived
- Pattern: whitelist
- References:
  - `python/fusion/pipeline.py:46-58`
  - `python/fusion/train_models.py:770-773`
  - `python/fusion/promote_to_cloud.py:172-173`
- Linked use cases: `UC-4`
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  - `pipeline.run_phase("train", dry_run=False, approve_training=False, ...)` results in training-blocking behavior.
  - `pipeline.run_phase("promote", dry_run=False, approve_promotion=False, ...)` results in promotion-blocking behavior.
  - Approved execution flags are passed intact through the pipeline dispatch boundary.

### REQ-005: Runtime external pull resilience on AI-first read paths
- Statement: User-facing AI-first routes that perform runtime trusted-market pulls must preserve explicit degraded-mode behavior and fallback metadata.
- Tier: 3
- Source type: code-derived
- References:
  - `app/api/strategy/posture/route.ts:142-169`
  - `app/api/sentiment/overview/route.ts:188-193`
  - `app/api/legislation/feed/route.ts:261-266`
  - `app/api/vegas/intel/route.ts:169-174`
- Linked use cases: `UC-5`
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  - Route handlers document and preserve snapshot-first or fallback semantics when trusted pulls fail.
  - Response payloads include metadata sufficient to identify degraded mode.
  - Runtime pull failures do not produce opaque success payloads without provenance.

### REQ-006: Operator documentation parity with V16 authority rules

## Use Cases
### UC-1: Serve intraday bars with executable fallback
- Actors: dashboard chart consumer, `/api/zl/intraday` route
- Preconditions: 15-minute table can be sparse while 1-minute table contains bars
- Flow:
  - Query `mkt.price_15m`
  - If unusable/empty, query `mkt.price_1m`
  - Return normalized envelope with accurate `source`
- Postconditions: route behavior matches declared fallback contract
- Requirement links: `REQ-001`

### UC-2.a: Target-zones route canonical envelope
- Actors: dashboard bootstrap loader
- Preconditions: latest `forecasts.target_zones` rows exist
- Flow:
  - Fetch `/api/zl/target-zones`
  - Parse canonical envelope contract
- Postconditions: payload is compatible with shared client contract
- Requirement links: `REQ-002`

### UC-2.b: Forecast-targets route canonical envelope
- Actors: probability surface loader
- Preconditions: latest `forecasts.target_zones` rows exist
- Flow:
  - Fetch `/api/zl/forecast-targets`
  - Parse same envelope contract as sibling route (or adapter-backed equivalent)
- Postconditions: route-level parser divergence is eliminated
- Requirement links: `REQ-002`

### UC-3: Record ingest run lifecycle with one vocabulary
- Actors: SQL ingest jobs, TS ingest helper, ops analytics readers
- Preconditions: ingest run starts and reaches terminal state
- Flow:
  - Write start lifecycle row
  - Update terminal status with canonical vocabulary
- Postconditions: status analytics are deterministic across producers
- Requirement links: `REQ-003`

### UC-4: Approval-gated training and promotion execution
- Actors: pipeline operator, train/promote phases
- Preconditions: non-dry execution requested
- Flow:
  - Dispatch phase through pipeline
  - Enforce explicit approval requirement
- Postconditions: unauthorized train/promote execution is blocked
- Requirement links: `REQ-004`

### UC-5: Degraded-mode transparency during runtime pull outages
- Actors: AI-first card route consumers
- Preconditions: runtime trusted-market pull fails or degrades
- Flow:
  - Route attempts pull
  - Route emits fallback output with provenance metadata
- Postconditions: consumers can distinguish degraded from fully fresh responses
- Requirement links: `REQ-005`

### UC-6: Operator startup documentation consistency
- Actors: maintainers and new operators
- Preconditions: onboarding/startup instructions are consulted
- Flow:
  - Read root/operator docs
  - Validate no conflict with authority startup constraints
- Postconditions: startup behavior does not rely on prohibited hardcoded-port assumptions
- Requirement links: `REQ-006`

### UC-7: Generate per-bug writeups at canonical path
- Actors: code review/spec audit phase outputs
- Preconditions: bug is confirmed
- Flow:
  - Create writeup file under `quality/writeups/`
- Postconditions: bug handoff artifact exists at canonical location
- Requirement links: `REQ-007`

### UC-8: Generate fix patch at canonical path
- Actors: reconciliation phase patch generation
- Preconditions: bug has proposed code fix
- Flow:
  - Emit `BUG-<id>-fix.patch` under `quality/patches/`
- Postconditions: fix patch path contract satisfied
- Requirement links: `REQ-008`

### UC-9: Generate regression-test patch at canonical path
- Actors: reconciliation phase patch generation
- Preconditions: bug has regression-test patch
- Flow:
  - Emit `BUG-<id>-regression-test.patch` under `quality/patches/`
- Postconditions: regression patch path contract satisfied
- Requirement links: `REQ-009`

### UC-10: Store code review outputs canonically
- Actors: Phase 3 code review executor
- Preconditions: pass outputs generated
- Flow:
  - Save review documents under `quality/code_reviews/`
- Postconditions: code-review artifacts are discoverable in canonical directory
- Requirement links: `REQ-010`

### UC-11: Store spec audit outputs canonically
- Actors: Phase 4 spec audit executor
- Preconditions: auditor and triage outputs generated
- Flow:
  - Save outputs under `quality/spec_audits/`
- Postconditions: spec-audit artifacts are discoverable in canonical directory
- Requirement links: `REQ-011`

### UC-12: Store sidecar JSON result outputs canonically
- Actors: Phase 4/5/6 executors
- Preconditions: sidecar result JSON produced
- Flow:
  - Save JSON results under `quality/results/`
- Postconditions: sidecar outputs are discoverable and gate-compatible
- Requirement links: `REQ-012`

### UC-13: Store and execute mechanical verification artifacts
- Actors: Phase 2/3/4 executors
- Preconditions: enumeration/dispatch contracts exist
- Flow:
  - Emit extraction artifacts under `quality/mechanical/`
  - Run `quality/mechanical/verify.sh`
- Postconditions: mechanical evidence artifacts are reproducible and validated
- Requirement links: `REQ-013`

### UC-14: Preserve canonical top-level quality layout
- Actors: all phase executors
- Preconditions: artifacts are being generated
- Flow:
  - Write artifacts to top-level `quality/<name>/`
  - Avoid creating `quality/workspace/`
- Postconditions: Phase 6 `check_no_workspace_dir` passes
- Requirement links: `REQ-014`

# Code Review Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Bootstrap
Read these artifacts before running Pass 1:
1. "'`quality/QUALITY.md`
2. `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`
3. `quality/CONTRACTS.md`
4. `quality/COVERAGE_MATRIX.md`
5. `quality/EXPLORATION.md`

## Pass 1: Structural Review
### Mandatory scrutiny sections
1. Input validation and boundary handling
2. Resource lifecycle
3. Concurrency and state management
4. Unit and encoding correctness
5. Enumeration and whitelist completeness

### Guardrails
- Line numbers are mandatory.
- Read full function bodies before raising a finding.
- Use `QUESTION` when uncertain, not `BUG`.
- Grep before claiming absence.
- Exclude style-only suggestions.

### Enumeration completeness mechanics
- Use existing `quality/mechanical/*_cases.txt` artifacts when available.
- If an artifact is missing, extract code-side lists with line-numbered entries before claiming completeness.
- Compare code-side list to spec/contract-side list and report diffs explicitly.

## Pass 2: Requirement Verification
For every REQ in `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`:
- Assign one verdict: `SATISFIED`, `VIOLATED`, `PARTIALLY SATISFIED`, or `NOT ASSESSABLE`.
- Provide at least one code citation per REQ.
- For REQs with per-site UCs (`UC-2.a`, `UC-2.b`), verify each site separately.
- For pattern-tagged REQs (`REQ-001`..`REQ-004`), do not skip evidence; include route/function-specific proof.

## Pass 3: Cross-Requirement Consistency
Compare REQ pairs sharing data contracts or policy boundaries:
- REQ-001 vs REQ-002: fallback behavior vs downstream envelope assumptions.
- REQ-002 vs REQ-005: route contract consistency vs runtime pull degradation semantics.
- REQ-003 vs REQ-010/REQ-011: telemetry vocabulary consistency vs review/audit artifact interpretation.
- REQ-004 vs REQ-013: approval gates vs mechanical verification of allowlists and dispatch boundaries.

## Output Format
Create one review artifact in `quality/code_reviews/` with sections:
- `## Pass 1: Structural Review`
- `## Pass 2: Requirement Verification`
- `## Pass 3: Cross-Requirement Consistency`
- `## Combined Summary`

Each finding entry format:
- `Source: <pass>`
- `Requirement: <REQ-NNN or N/A>`
- `Location: <path:line>`
- `Verdict: BUG | QUESTION | VIOLATED | PARTIALLY SATISFIED | INCONSISTENT`
- `Impact: HIGH | MEDIUM | LOW`
- `Evidence: <quoted or paraphrased code behavior>`
- `Regression test linkage: <test name or exemption>`

## Closure Rules
- Every confirmed BUG must map to a regression test in `quality/test_regression.*` or an explicit exemption.
- For every requirement violation, include expected vs actual behavior.
- If a finding is overturned during spec audit triage, remove/reclassify its regression test.

# Spec Audit Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Council Setup
Run three independent auditors with no shared findings until triage:
- Auditor A: requirement-first strict contract verification
- Auditor B: architecture consistency and cross-file behavior verification
- Auditor C: adversarial boundary and omission-focused verification

## Inputs
1. "'`quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`
2. `quality/QUALITY.md`
3. `quality/CONTRACTS.md`
4. `quality/COVERAGE_MATRIX.md`
5. Relevant source files cited by each REQ

## Output Locations
- Auditor reports: `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor-1.md` .. `-3.md`
- Triage synthesis: `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-triage.md`
- Probe script: `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.sh`
- Probe output capture: `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.out.txt`

## Audit Procedure
1. Each auditor reviews all REQs independently and records per-REQ verdicts with code citations.
2. Triage compares overlaps, disagreements, and net-new findings.
3. Every confirmation or rejection using a probe must be executable evidence:
   - Write assertions in `triage_probes.sh` or `quality/mechanical/verify.sh`.
   - Execute probes and capture output file.
4. Classify each finding as:
   - `Real code bug`
   - `Spec gap`
   - `False positive`
   - `Needs follow-up`

## Mandatory Finding Fields
Each triage finding includes:
- `id` (`BUG-NNN` if confirmed)
- `requirement` (`REQ-NNN`)
- `source` (`code-spec` | `internal-prose` | `cross-source`)
- `severity` (`HIGH` | `MEDIUM` | `LOW`)
- `evidence` (file:line and/or probe output)
- `disposition` candidate

## Post-Triage Hooks
- Confirmed code bugs feed Phase 5 regression test workflow.
- Confirmed spec gaps feed requirement/spec update queue.
- Overturned code-review findings must be reconciled with regression artifacts.

/bin/zsh -lc "cat > quality/RUN_TDD_TESTS.md <<'EOF'
# TDD Verification Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.3 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Purpose
Validate every confirmed bug with a red/green cycle and produce patch-ready evidence without mutating source outside "'`quality/`.

## Inputs
- `quality/BUGS.md`
- `quality/patches/BUG-<id>-regression-test.patch`
- Optional `quality/patches/BUG-<id>-fix.patch`
- Project test command(s)

## Procedure Per Bug
1. Red phase:
   - Apply regression-test patch in disposable worktree.
   - Disable skip/xfail guard for this run.
   - Run targeted regression test.
   - Expect failure.
2. Green phase:
   - Apply fix patch (if present) plus regression-test patch.
   - Re-run targeted regression test.
   - Expect pass.
3. Record outcomes in sidecar JSON.

## Output Files
- `quality/results/tdd-results.json` (`schema_version: "1.1"`, `skill_version: "1.5.7"`)
- `quality/results/recheck-results.json` (`schema_version: "1.0"`)
- Bug writeups in `quality/writeups/`

## Required Sidecar Fields
`tdd-results.json` must include:
- `schema_version`, `skill_version`, `date`, `project`
- `bugs_total`, `bugs_verified`, `bugs_open`
- `results[]` with `bug_id`, `red_phase`, `green_phase`, `verdict`, `regression_test`, `fix_patch`, `writeup_path`

## Verdict Rules
- `TDD verified`: red fails, green passes
- `confirmed open`: red fails, green skipped (no fix patch)
- `needs investigation`: red passes unexpectedly or test misalignment detected

## Guardrails
- Do not apply patches to working source tree directly.
- Use disposable worktree for destructive apply/run steps.
- Keep skip/xfail guards restored after verification runs.

class TrainingReadinessError(RuntimeError):

def _parse_csv(value: str | None, default: tuple[str, ...]) -> tuple[str, ...]:
    if not value:
        return default
    parsed = tuple(item.strip().upper() for item in value.split(",") if item.strip())
    return parsed or default


def _parse_float(value: str | None, default: float) -> float:
    if not value:
        return default
    return float(value)


def _as_utc_datetime(value: Any) -> datetime | None:
    if value is None:
        return None
    if isinstance(value, datetime):
        return value.astimezone(timezone.utc) if value.tzinfo else value.replace(tzinfo=timezone.utc)
    if isinstance(value, date):
        return datetime(value.year, value.month, value.day, tzinfo=timezone.utc)
    if isinstance(value, str):
        parsed = pd.to_datetime(value, errors="coerce", utc=True)
        if pd.isna(parsed):
            return None
        return parsed.to_pydatetime()
    return None


def _age_hours(value: Any, now_utc: datetime) -> float | None:
    dt = _as_utc_datetime(value)
    if dt is None:
        return None
    return (now_utc - dt).total_seconds() / 3600.0


def _age_days(value: Any, now_utc: datetime) -> float | None:
    hours = _age_hours(value, now_utc)
    if hours is None:
        return None
    return hours / 24.0


def _ratio(numerator: int, denominator: int) -> float:
    if denominator <= 0:
        return 0.0
    return float(numerator) / float(denominator)


def _format_issues(issues: list[str]) -> str:
    if len(issues) <= _ISSUE_PREVIEW_LIMIT:
        return "; ".join(issues)
    shown = "; ".join(issues[:_ISSUE_PREVIEW_LIMIT])
    return f"{shown}; ... {len(issues) - _ISSUE_PREVIEW_LIMIT} more"


def _table_exists(cur: Any, *, schema: str, table: str) -> bool:
    cur.execute(
        """
        SELECT EXISTS (
          SELECT 1
          FROM information_schema.tables
          WHERE table_schema = %s AND table_name = %s
        )
        """,
        (schema, table),
    )
    return bool(cur.fetchone()[0])


def _column_exists(cur: Any, *, schema: str, table: str, column: str) -> bool:
    cur.execute(
        """
        SELECT EXISTS (
          SELECT 1
          FROM information_schema.columns
          WHERE table_schema = %s AND table_name = %s AND column_name = %s
        )
        """,
        (schema, table, column),
    )
    return bool(cur.fetchone()[0])


def _load_contract() -> TrainingGateContract:
    enforce_parity = os.getenv("TRAINING_ENFORCE_CLOUD_LOCAL_PARITY", "0").strip().lower()
    single_matrix = os.getenv("TRAINING_SINGLE_MATRIX_CONTRACT", "1").strip().lower()
    require_options = os.getenv("TRAINING_REQUIRE_OPTIONS", "0").strip().lower()
    return TrainingGateContract(
        required_symbols=_parse_csv(
            os.getenv("TRAINING_REQUIRED_SYMBOLS"),
            (),
        ),
        required_fred_series=_parse_csv(
            os.getenv("TRAINING_REQUIRED_FRED_SERIES"),

        ),
        min_daily_rows_per_symbol=int(os.getenv("TRAINING_MIN_DAILY_ROWS_PER_SYMBOL", "250")),

        min_fred_series=int(os.getenv("TRAINING_MIN_FRED_SERIES", "50")),
        min_fred_rows=int(os.getenv("TRAINING_MIN_FRED_ROWS", "500000")),
        min_weather_series=int(os.getenv("TRAINING_MIN_WEATHER_SERIES", "4")),
        min_weather_rows=int(os.getenv("TRAINING_MIN_WEATHER_ROWS", "500000")),

from __future__ import annotations

import re
import unittest
from pathlib import Path
from unittest.mock import patch

from fusion import pipeline

ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]


def read_text(relative_path: str) -> str:
    return (ROOT / relative_path).read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")


class SpecRequirementTests(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_req_001_intraday_route_contains_executable_1m_fallback(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-001] intraday route must execute 15m->1m fallback.\"\"\"
        source = read_text(\"app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts\")
        self.assertIn(\"Try 15-minute bars first, fall back to 1-minute\", source)
        self.assertIn('.from(\"price_15m\")', source)
        self.assertIn(
            '.from(\"price_1m\")',
            source,
            \"REQ-001 violation: 1-minute fallback query path is not implemented.\",
        )

    def test_req_002_forecast_target_routes_share_api_envelope_contract(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-002] equivalent target routes should share envelope semantics.\"\"\"
        target_zones = read_text(\"app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts\")
        forecast_targets = read_text(\"app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts\")
        self.assertIn(\"ok: true\", target_zones)
        self.assertIn(\"data:\", target_zones)
        self.assertIn(\"asOf:\", target_zones)
        self.assertIn(
            \"ok: true\",
            forecast_targets,
            \"REQ-002 violation: forecast-targets route does not emit canonical envelope keys.\",
        )
        self.assertIn(\"data:\", forecast_targets)
        self.assertIn(\"asOf:\", forecast_targets)

    def test_req_003_ingest_status_vocab_is_canonical_across_writers(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-003] all ingest writers should share one status vocabulary.\"\"\"
        helper = read_text(\"lib/server/ingest-run.ts\")
        sql_intraday = read_text(\"supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql\")
        sql_fill = read_text(\"supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql\")

        helper_statuses = set(re.findall(r'status:\\s*\"([A-Z_]+)\"', helper))
        sql_statuses = set(re.findall(r\"status\\s*:=\\s*'([a-z_]+)'\", sql_intraday + \"\\n\" + sql_fill))
        self.assertTrue(helper_statuses, \"Expected TS helper status literals to be present.\")
        self.assertTrue(sql_statuses, \"Expected SQL status literals to be present.\")

        normalized_sql = {s.upper() for s in sql_statuses}
        self.assertSetEqual(
            helper_statuses,
            normalized_sql,
            \"REQ-003 violation: SQL and TS status vocabularies are not canonicalized to one set.\",
        )

    def test_req_004_train_phase_requires_explicit_approval(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-004] train dispatch must propagate explicit approval flag.\"\"\"
        captured: dict[str, object] = {}

        def fake_train(*, dry_run: bool, approved: bool) -> dict[str, object]:
            captured[\"dry_run\"] = dry_run
            captured[\"approved\"] = approved
            return {\"phase\": \"train\", \"approved\": approved, \"dry_run\": dry_run}

        with patch.dict(pipeline.PHASE_MAP, {\"train\": fake_train}, clear=False):
            result = pipeline.run_phase(
                \"train\",
                dry_run=False,
                approve_training=False,
                approve_promotion=False,
            )

        self.assertEqual(result[\"phase\"], \"train\")
        self.assertFalse(captured[\"approved\"])
        self.assertFalse(captured[\"dry_run\"])

    def test_req_004_promote_phase_requires_explicit_approval(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-004] promote dispatch must force dry_run when unapproved.\"\"\"
        captured: dict[str, object] = {}

        def fake_promote(*, dry_run: bool, approved: bool) -> dict[str, object]:
            captured[\"dry_run\"] = dry_run
            captured[\"approved\"] = approved
            return {\"phase\": \"promote\", \"approved\": approved, \"dry_run\": dry_run}

        with patch.dict(pipeline.PHASE_MAP, {\"promote\": fake_promote}, clear=False):
            result = pipeline.run_phase(
                \"promote\",
                dry_run=False,
                approve_training=False,
                approve_promotion=False,
            )

        self.assertEqual(result[\"phase\"], \"promote\")
        self.assertFalse(captured[\"approved\"])
        self.assertTrue(captured[\"dry_run\"])

    def test_req_005_runtime_pull_routes_include_fallback_language(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-005] AI-first routes should expose fallback/degraded behavior.\"\"\"
        strategy = read_text(\"app/api/strategy/posture/route.ts\")
        sentiment = read_text(\"app/api/sentiment/overview/route.ts\")
        legislation = read_text(\"app/api/legislation/feed/route.ts\")
        vegas = read_text(\"app/api/vegas/intel/route.ts\")

        joined = \"\\n\".join([strategy, sentiment, legislation, vegas]).lower()
        self.assertRegex(joined, r\"fallback|snapshot|degraded\")

    def test_req_006_readme_does_not_hardcode_localhost_3000(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-006] operator docs should avoid prohibited hardcoded-port guidance.\"\"\"
        readme = read_text(\"README.md\").lower()
        self.assertNotIn(\"localhost:3000\", readme)

    def test_req_007_writeup_path_requirement_statement_present(self) -> None:
        reqs = read_text(\"quality/REQUIREMENTS.md\")
        self.assertIn(\"Per-bug writeups are placed at quality/writeups/BUG-<id>.md.\", reqs)

    def test_req_008_fix_patch_path_requirement_statement_present(self) -> None:
        reqs = read_text(\"quality/REQUIREMENTS.md\")
        self.assertIn(\"Fix patches are placed at quality/patches/BUG-<id>-fix.patch.\", reqs)

    def test_req_009_regression_patch_path_requirement_statement_present(self) -> None:
        reqs = read_text(\"quality/REQUIREMENTS.md\")
        self.assertIn(\"Regression-test patches are placed at quality/patches/BUG-<id>-regression-test.patch.\", reqs)

    def test_req_010_code_review_path_requirement_statement_present(self) -> None:
        reqs = read_text(\"quality/REQUIREMENTS.md\")
        self.assertIn(\"Code review output is placed at quality/code_reviews/.\", reqs)

    def test_req_011_spec_audit_path_requirement_statement_present(self) -> None:
        reqs = read_text(\"quality/REQUIREMENTS.md\")
        self.assertIn(\"Spec audit outputs (auditor reports + triage) are placed at quality/spec_audits/.\", reqs)

    def test_req_012_sidecar_results_path_requirement_statement_present(self) -> None:
        reqs = read_text(\"quality/REQUIREMENTS.md\")
        self.assertIn(
            \"Sidecar JSON results (tdd-results.json, integration-results.json, recheck-results.json) are placed at quality/results/.\",
            reqs,
        )

    def test_req_013_mechanical_path_requirement_statement_present(self) -> None:
        reqs = read_text(\"quality/REQUIREMENTS.md\")
        self.assertIn(\"Mechanical-verification artifacts (verify.sh + *_cases.txt) are placed at quality/mechanical/.\", reqs)

    def test_req_014_workspace_forbidden_requirement_statement_present(self) -> None:
        reqs = read_text(\"quality/REQUIREMENTS.md\")
        self.assertIn(\"quality/workspace/<name>/ is forbidden\", reqs)


class FitnessScenarioTests(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_scenario_1_intraday_source_field_not_hardcoded_when_fallback_needed(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-001] fallback-capable routes should not hardcode one source label.\"\"\"
        source = read_text(\"app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts\")
        self.assertNotIn(
            'source: \"mkt.price_15m\"',
            source,
            \"Scenario 1 risk: source label is hardcoded despite fallback contract.\",
        )

    def test_scenario_2_forecast_overlay_gate_is_not_hard_disabled(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-002] chart target-zone rendering should not be globally disabled.\"\"\"
        chart = read_text(\"components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx\")
        self.assertIn(\"SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY = true\", chart)

    def test_scenario_3_probability_surface_and_dashboard_share_contract_path(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-002] equivalent consumers should not require route-specific parsers.\"\"\"
        surface = read_text(\"components/dashboard/ProbabilitySurface.tsx\")
        dashboard = read_text(\"app/(protected)/dashboard/page.tsx\")
        self.assertIn(\"/api/zl/target-zones\", dashboard)
        self.assertNotIn(
            \"/api/zl/forecast-targets\",
            surface,
            \"Scenario 3 risk: probability surface still depends on divergent endpoint contract.\",
        )

    def test_scenario_4_ingest_status_values_do_not_split_case_domains(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-003] case-domain drift in status values should be absent.\"\"\"
        helper = read_text(\"lib/server/ingest-run.ts\")
        self.assertNotRegex(helper, r'\"SUCCESS\"|\"FAILED\"|\"RUNNING\"')

    def test_scenario_5_train_models_contains_explicit_approval_guard(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-004] train_models should enforce explicit approval check.\"\"\"
        train_source = read_text(\"python/fusion/train_models.py\")
        self.assertIn(\"if not approved:\", train_source)
        self.assertIn(\"Training requires explicit approval\", train_source)

    def test_scenario_6_routes_document_snapshot_and_trusted_pull_order(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-005] runtime pull routes should expose snapshot/degraded semantics.\"\"\"
        strategy = read_text(\"app/api/strategy/posture/route.ts\").lower()
        self.assertRegex(strategy, r\"snapshot|fallback\")

    def test_scenario_7_snapshot_allowlist_is_not_empty(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-004] trusted snapshot sources list should be non-empty.\"\"\"
        snapshot = read_text(\"lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts\")
        entries = re.findall(r'\"([a-z0-9\\-]+)\"', snapshot.split(\"TRUSTED_SNAPSHOT_SOURCES\", 1)[1])
        self.assertGreaterEqual(len(entries), 4)

    def test_scenario_8_readme_drift_is_detectable(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: code-derived — REQ-006] README should align with authority startup guidance.\"\"\"
        readme = read_text(\"README.md\")
        agents = read_text(\"AGENTS.md\")
        self.assertNotIn(\"localhost:3000\", readme)
        self.assertIn(\"No hardcoded port 3000\", agents)


class BoundaryAndEdgeCaseTests(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_boundary_intraday_tables_exist_in_migration_contract(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — from mkt schema tables] both intraday table levels exist.\"\"\"
        migration = read_text(\"supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql\")
        self.assertIn(\"create table if not exists mkt.price_15m\", migration.lower())
        self.assertIn(\"create table if not exists mkt.price_1m\", migration.lower())

    def test_boundary_horizon_allowlist_parity_across_routes(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-002 parity pattern] horizon allowlist should match across forecast routes.\"\"\"
        forecast = read_text(\"app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts\")
        target = read_text(\"app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts\")
        targets = read_text(\"app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts\")

        pattern = re.compile(r\"AG_HORIZON_DAYS\\s*=\\s*\\[30,\\s*90,\\s*180\\]\")
        self.assertRegex(forecast, pattern)
        self.assertRegex(target, pattern)
        self.assertRegex(targets, pattern)

    def test_boundary_legacy_horizon_map_parity_across_routes(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-002 parity pattern] legacy remap should match across forecast routes.\"\"\"
        expected_pairs = [\"7: 30\", \"14: 90\", \"30: 180\"]
        for rel in [
            \"app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts\",
            \"app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts\",
            \"app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts\",
        ]:
            text = read_text(rel)
            for pair in expected_pairs:
                self.assertIn(pair, text)

    def test_boundary_trusted_snapshot_sources_are_exactly_expected_set(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — snapshot allowlist] trusted source list should match expected identifiers.\"\"\"
        source = read_text(\"lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts\")
        values = set(
            re.findall(r'\"(trusted-live-pull|trusted-authority-pull|ai-daily-refresh|chatgpt-pro-subscription-refresh)\"', source)
        )
        self.assertSetEqual(
            values,
            {
                \"trusted-live-pull\",
                \"trusted-authority-pull\",
                \"ai-daily-refresh\",
                \"chatgpt-pro-subscription-refresh\",
            },
        )

    def test_boundary_overlay_attach_and_detach_paths_match_gate(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — chart overlay lifecycle] attach/detach should both be gated consistently.\"\"\"
        chart = read_text(\"components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx\")
        attach_gated = \"if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {\\n      series.attachPrimitive(forecastTargetsPrimitive);\" in chart
        detach_gated = \"if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {\\n          series.detachPrimitive(forecastTargetsPrimitive);\" in chart
        self.assertTrue(attach_gated)
        self.assertTrue(detach_gated)

    def test_boundary_pipeline_dispatch_train_passes_approved_flag(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — run_phase dispatch] train dispatch passes approval argument through.\"\"\"
        captured: dict[str, object] = {}

        def fake_train(*, dry_run: bool, approved: bool) -> dict[str, object]:
            captured[\"dry_run\"] = dry_run
            captured[\"approved\"] = approved
            return {\"ok\": True}

        with patch.dict(pipeline.PHASE_MAP, {\"train\": fake_train}, clear=False):
            pipeline.run_phase(
                \"train\",
                dry_run=True,
                approve_training=True,
                approve_promotion=False,
            )

        self.assertTrue(captured[\"dry_run\"])
        self.assertTrue(captured[\"approved\"])

#"'!/usr/bin/env bash
# Generated by Quality Playbook v1.5.7 — https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook
# Author: Andrew Stellman · Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

ROOT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../.." && pwd)"
cd "$ROOT_DIR"

status=0

compare_artifact() {
  local expected_file="$1"
  local extractor="$2"
  local tmp
  tmp="$(mktemp)"
  trap '"'rm -f \""'$tmp"'"' RETURN

  eval \""'$extractor" > "$tmp"
  if ! diff -u "$expected_file" "$tmp"; then
    echo "FAIL: artifact mismatch -> $expected_file"
    status=1
  else
    echo "PASS: $expected_file"
  fi

  rm -f "$tmp"
  trap - RETURN
}

  \"quality/mechanical/forecast_normalize_horizon_cases.txt\" \\
  \"awk '/const AG_HORIZON_DAYS/ {in_block=1} in_block && /\\\\[30, 90, 180\\\\]|7: 30|14: 90|30: 180/ {line=\\"'$0; gsub(/''^[[:space:]]+/, '"\\\"\\\", line); print line} in_block && /};/ {exit}' app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts\"

  exit "$status"
